If it is true that what makes fantasy is the idea of different rules,
then that would explain why Star Wars sits so uncomfortably (but
fantasy trappings of space opera, but we are in no doubt that we are being told
a fairy tale. When we see those words “A long time ago, in a galaxy
far, far away …” we don’t think “Hang on, all galaxies are far away. I
mean the nearest galaxy to us is Andromeda, and that’s 2,500,000 light
years away.” What we think is “Once upon a time …” and what we
understand is “The rules are different here.”
